originall synne ❧ appereth suffyciently subtyle argumēt broght forthe scoles nat counsell cesar albeit cauillacion may easely auoyded yet al good men may se teache none inconuenyence thys behalfe fyrste requyre cōfession harde diligētly marked shall delyuer v suspicion straūge doctryne▪ wrytten thus ❧ trāslated duche teache falle adam euery man naturally borne cōceiued syn borne al wombe nat done without peculiar gyfte ayde grace name gyftꝭ expressly thynge may vnderstāde notice god feare truste towarde god appereth olde definicion dothe speake thyng detractyng plucking away feare god hope say nat actual dedes also gyftes myght sentence hathe definicyon austyne vsethe define originall synne concupiscence meaneth whē iustice loste concupiscence succeded decayed nature nat feare loue truste god seketh loueth carnall thynges iudgement god thys sycke corrupte nature eyther voyde feare despyseth beynge replenyshed feare hateth thus austyne compriseth aswele defaulte faylyng viciouse qualitie whiche therof ensueth cōcupiscēce nat corruptiō quality bodie also vnryght turnyng thyngꝭ carnal ye superiour power se nat saye whiche bothe attribute man concupiscence nat mortified holy ghoste also loue god aboue althyngꝭ therfore haue ryghtly expressed bothe two description original synne saye defautes nat power beleue god nat power dreade loue god also haue concupiscence whiche agaynste worde god seketh carnalitie say seketh nat corporal pleasure also carnal wysdome iustice hathe confidence worldly goodes contemnyng god nat onely olde late doctours namely iudgemēt teache original synne aswel lackes defaultes haue remembred concupiscence luste thus saythe saynt thomas peccatum originis habet priuationē originalis iusticie cum hoc inordinatam dispositionem partium anime vnde non est priuatio pura sed quidam • abitus corruptus originall synne saythe thomas hathe priuacyon originall iustice inordinate disposicion partꝭ soule nat pure •• pro viribus quas dominus donare dignatur colligimꝰ non iustificare • ominem preceptis bone vite nisi per fidem iesa christi therfore consydered handled accordyng power whiche god vouchsaueth gyue v repeteth epystles 4 chap romanes sayeth thus operanti merces non imputatur secundum graci • sed secundum debitum ei autem qui non operatur credit autem eum qui iustificat impium reputatur fides eius ad iusticiam worketh geuē rewarde nat fauour dutie cōtrary wyse worketh nat trusteth hym iustifieth wycked hys beleue accompted ryghtwysnes clerely pronounceth faythe accompted ryghtwysenes faythe thynge whiche god pronounceth ryghtwysnes addeth frely imputed denieth frely imputed shuld due workes ergo also excluded merite morall workes due iustifycacion god faythe shuld nat accompted ryghwysenes without workes sayeth▪ saye fayth īputed abrahā ryghtwysnes fyfthe chapitre sayeth iustifyed fayth haue peace towarde god haue quyet glad conscience god rom 10 harte beleued ryghtwysnes sayth hys epystle ireneus thus subditus autem mundus eo per legem factus est quia ex prescripto legis omnes conueniuntur et ex operibus legis nemo iustificatur saynte ambrose id est quia per legem peccatum cognoscitur sed culpa non relaxatur videbatur lex nocuisse que omnes fecerat peccatores sed veniens dominus iesus peccatuz omnibꝰ quod nemo poterat euitare donauit et chirographum nostrū sui sanguinis effusione deleuit hoc est quod ait abundauit peccatū per legem superabundauit autem gratia per iesum quia postquā totus mundus subditus factus est totius mūdi peccatum abstulit sicut testificatus est iohannes dicēs ecce agnus dei ecce qui tollit peccatū mundi et ideo nemo glorietur operibus quia nemo factis suis instificatur sed qui instus est donatum habet quia post lauacrum iustificatus est fides ergo est que liberat per sanguinem christi quia beatus ille cui peccatum remittitur et venia donatur saye world made subiect therfore lawe prescript lawe al conuented hyghe iudge workes lawe mā iustifyed lawe synne knowen offence remytted lawe semed haue hurted whiche made men synners lorde iesus comyng pardoned unto al men synne whiche man coulde eschewe dyd clene stryke chirografe shedyng blode thys sayeth syn aboundaunt lawe grace iesus aboundant hole worlde become subiecte toke away sinne hole worlde testifieth iohan saing lo lambe god lo taketh awaye syn worlde therfore lette man glorye hys workes man iustyfyed hy hys factes iustifyed hath gyuen wherfore fayth thynge delyuereth bloude chryste blyssed synne remytted pardone gyuen wordes saynt ambrose legis quod fieri non potest sed per fidem concilians iustificatorem perueniat et faciat et viuat eam opus rectum quod qui fecerit viuit eo non fit nisi iustificato iustificatio autem ex fide wherfore may nat affyrme god reputed iust owne fulfyllyng lawe muste thynke recoūpted iust acceptable christe nat lawe workes imperfecte inchoate fulfyllyng lawe pleaseth god christe also fayth dissimula • io ꝑniciosa quae enim fiducia est ei quā periculū non attendit • au • quod ibi timoris remedium ubi nec timor sentitur nec materia ipsa timori • • fiducia solacium est nec eget ille solatio qui laetatur cum male fecerit pessimis rebus magi exultat rogemus ita que fratres responderi nobis quātas habeamus iniquitates peccata scelera nostra delicta • nobis desideremus ostendi partely also disagree gospel furthermore expounyng scripture playe deuise soeuer lyste confutation doctrine chiefeste cause offence peryllous whiche saynte iohn̄ chiefely complaynethe apocalypseapo 17 whan describeth kyngdome pope whan shall come superstition religious ꝑsones whiche infinite howe many greuous offensions applyenge merites deade body huryed habite religion furthermore none occasion
